    static settings(): iq_camera_settings {
      let result = $mol_state_local.value('camera_settings') as iq_camera_settings | null
      if (result === null) {
        const response = $iq_fetch.json( '/visca_settings_manager/get_settings' ) as {
          "data" : iq_camera_settings
        }
        result = response.data
        $mol_state_local.value('camera_settings', result)
      }
      return result
    }
    
    static upload_settings(body: object) {
      $iq_fetch.post( '/visca_settings_manager/upload_settings', body)
      $mol_state_local.value('camera_settings', null)
    }

$mssc_dash_pane_main $mol_plot_pane
  gap_hor 0
  gap_vert 0
  allow_draw false
  event *
    ^
    click? <=> event_click? <=> click? null
    pointerdown? <=> event_start? null
    pointermove? <=> event_move? null


  export class $mssc_dash_pane_main extends $.$mssc_dash_pane_main {
    protected moved = false

    override event_start() {
      this.moved = false
    }

    override event_move() {
      this.moved = true
    }

    override event_click(e?: Event) {
      if (this.moved) return
      return this.click(e)
    }
  }

    protected scrolled = false

    @ $mol_mem
    scroll_to_selected() {
      if (this.scrolled) return false

      const id = this.spread()
      const item = id ? this.Menu_link3(id) : null
      if (! item ) return false

      const menu = this.Menu_links()

      const path = menu.view_find( v => v === item ).next().value
      menu.force_render( new Set( path ) )

      const top = item.view_rect()?.top ?? 0

      if ( top ) {
        this.Menu().Body().dom_node().scrollTo({ top })

        this.scrolled = true
      }

      return this.scrolled
    }

    auto_scroll_to_active() {
      try {
        this.scroll_to_selected()
      } catch (e) {
        $mol_fail_log(e)
      }

      return null
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    current_item_rendered() {
      const id = this.spread()
      const item = id ? this.Menu_link3(id) : null
      if (! item) return null

      const menu = this.Menu_links()
      const path = menu.view_find( v => v === item ).next().value
      menu.force_render( new Set( path ) )
      return item
    }

    protected scrolled = false
    @ $mol_mem
    scroll_to_selected() {
      if (this.scrolled) return false

      const item = this.current_item_rendered()
      if (! item ) return false

      const item_rect = item.view_rect()
      const scroll_body_rect = this.Menu().Body().view_rect()

      if ( ! item_rect?.top || ! scroll_body_rect ) return false

      const gap = 0
      const top = item_rect.top - scroll_body_rect.top + item_rect.height + gap

      this.Menu().Body().dom_node().scrollTo({ top })

      this.scrolled = true

      return true
    }

    @ $mol_action
    static blob_safe( path: string, init?: $yuf_transport_req ) {
      try {
        return this.get( path, init ).blob()
      } catch (e) {
        if ($mol_promise_like(e)) $mol_fail_hidden(e)
        if (e instanceof $yuf_transport_error && e.cause?.http_code === 404) return null
        $mol_fail_hidden(e)
      }
    }

  pointerDown(e) {
    if (e.defaultPrevented) return
    e.preventDefault()
    e.target.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId)
    this.active(true)
  }

  pointerMove(e) {
    if (e.defaultPrevented) return
    e.preventDefault()
    if (!this.active()) return

    this.position({
      x: Math.ceil(e.offsetX),
      y: Math.ceil(e.offsetY),
    })
  }

  pointerUp(e) {
    if (e.defaultPrevented) return
    e.preventDefault()
    this.active(false)
  }

    point_in_polygon([x, y]: readonly [x: number, y: number], points: (readonly [x: number, y: number])[]) {
      // ray-casting algorithm based on
      // https://wrf.ecse.rpi.edu/Research/Short_Notes/pnpoly.html

      let inside = false

      for (let i = 0, j = points.length - 1; i < points.length; j = i++) {
        const [ xi, yi ] = points[i]
        const [ xj, yj ] = points[j]

        const intersect = ((yi > y) != (yj > y))
          && (x < (xj - xi) * (y - yi) / (yj - yi) + xi)

        if (intersect) inside = ! inside
      }

      return inside
    }

    event() : { [ key : string ] : ( event : Event )=> void } {
      return {}

    @ $mol_mem
    event_fiberized() {
      return new Proxy(this.event(), {
        get(target, key) {
          if (typeof target[key as keyof typeof target] === 'function') {
            return function faberized(e: Event) {
              const event = $mol_wire_sync(e)
              return target[key as keyof typeof target](event)
            }
          }

          return target[key as keyof typeof target]
        }
      })
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    event_async() {
      return { ... $mol_wire_async(this.event_fiberized()) }
    }

    override option_hint(id: string) {
      return this.icons()[id] && this.icon_only()
        ? this.option_title(id)
        : super.option_hint(id)
    }

    override option_label( id: string ) {
      const label = super.option_label(id)

      const icon = this.icons()[id]
      if (icon) {
        return this.icon_only() ? [ icon ] : [ icon, ...label ]
      }

      return label
    }

    static full_path(path: string) {
      const { origin, pathname } = this.$.$mol_dom_context.location

      if ( path.match(/^[\w:]?\/\//) ) return path
      if ( path.startsWith('/') ) return `${origin}${path}`

      let base = pathname.replace(/[^\/]+\.html?$/, '')
      if (! base.endsWith('/')) base += '/'

      return `${origin}${base}${path}`
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    opened_ensure() {
      $mol_wire_sync(this).open(true)
      return {
        destructor: () => this.open(false)
      }
    }

    open(next: boolean) {
      const id = this.id()
      const open = this.factory().open_task_synced(id)
      return open(next)
    }

    @ $mol_mem_key
    static open_task_synced(screening_id: string) {
      $mol_wire_solid()
      const host = this.$.$mol_wire_async( this )
      return (next: boolean) => host.opened_task(screening_id, next)
    }
